  <script>
   var querystring = window.location.search;
  
        //Every request to omniture cost the business money so we dont want to
        //track pages that do meta refreshes
        if (querystring !== "?reloaded=true") {
            requirejs(['omniture'], function (omniture) {
  
                var aamGetCookie = function (c_name) {
                    var i, x, y, c = document.cookie.split(";");
                    for (i = 0; i < c.length; i++) {
                        x = c[i].substr(0, c[i].indexOf("="));
                        y = c[i].substr(c[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
                        x = x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
                        if (x == c_name)
                        {
                            return unescape(y);
                        }
                    }
                };
  
                var tracking = '';
                var cookie = aamGetCookie("interactive");
                var interactive = (cookie) ? JSON.parse(cookie) : {};
  
                if (interactive.tid) {
                    tracking = interactive.tid;
                }
  
                var omnitureInitiated = false;
  
                var initAnalytics = function(targetData) {
  
                    if(omnitureInitiated) {
                        return;
                    }
  
                    omnitureInitiated = true;
  
                    omnitureData = {
                        trackingId: tracking,
                        site: "sky/portal/sports",
                        section: "home",
                        contentType: "home",
                        contentId: "",
                        sport: "None",
                        account: "bskybsports",
                        headline: "",
                        storyType: ""
                    };
  
                    var omnitureDataChecked = {
                        fixtureDetails: ""
                    };
  
                    Object.keys(omnitureDataChecked).forEach(key => {
                       if (omnitureDataChecked[key]) {
                           omnitureData[key] = omnitureDataChecked[key];
                       }
                    });
  
                    if(typeof targetData !== "undefined" && targetData.tntVal) {
                        omnitureData.tnt = targetData.tntVal;
                    }
  
                    var additionalSection = "";
  
                    if (additionalSection) {
                        var formattedAdditionalSection = additionalSection.replace(/-/g,"_");
                        omnitureData.section = omnitureData.section + '/' + formattedAdditionalSection;
                    }
  
                    // site-wide analytics
                    omniture.init(omnitureData);
                };
  
                if (window.sdc && window.sdc.pubSub) {
                    window.sdc.pubSub.subscribe('dynamic-tile.events.adobe-target-fetched', function(data) {
                        initAnalytics(data);
                    });
                }
  
                setTimeout(initAnalytics, 2000);
            });
        }
  </script>
